Evaluate the following integral using the Cauchy Integral Formula: $\int_{|z|=1} \frac{2z^3-5z+1}{(z-1)^2} \,dz$ Hint: The Cauchy Integral Formula states that if $f(z)$ is analytic in a region containing a simple, positively oriented closed contour $C$ and if $z_0$ is any point interior to that contour, then $\oint_C \frac{f(z)}{z-z_0} \,dz = 2\pi i f(z_0)$.
<think> Alright, I need to evaluate the integral \[ \int_{|z|=1} \frac{2z^3 - 5z + 1}{(z - 1)^2} \, dz \] using the Cauchy Integral Formula. First, let's recall what the Cauchy Integral Formula states. It says that if \( f(z) \) is analytic in a region containing a simple, positively oriented closed contour \( C \), and if \( z_0 \) is any point interior to that contour, then \[ \oint_C \frac{f(z)}{z - z_0} \, dz = 2\pi i f(z_0). \] In this problem, our contour \( C \) is the unit circle \( |z| = 1 \). We need to determine if there are any singularities of the integrand inside this contour. The integrand is \[ \frac{2z^3 - 5z + 1}{(z - 1)^2}. \] The denominator \( (z - 1)^2 \) has a pole at \( z = 1 \). Now, we need to check whether this pole lies inside or outside the contour \( |z| = 1 \). Plugging in \( z = 1 \), we have \( |1| = 1 \), so the pole is exactly on the contour. However, the Cauchy Integral Formula applies when the singularity is **inside** the contour, not on it. Therefore, since \( z = 1 \) lies on the contour, we cannot directly apply the standard Cauchy Integral Formula. But wait, maybe there's a way to adjust for the pole being on the contour. Perhaps we can use the residue theorem instead, which generalizes the Cauchy Integral Formula to include poles on the contour. The residue theorem states that for a function with isolated singularities inside a simple closed contour, \[ \oint_C f(z) \, dz = 2\pi i \sum \text{Res}(f, z_k), \] where the sum is over all singularities \( z_k \) inside \( C \). Let's proceed with the residue theorem. Our integrand has a double pole at \( z = 1 \). To find the residue at this pole, we'll need to compute the first derivative of the numerator evaluated at \( z = 1 \), since the residue for a pole of order \( n \) is given by \[ \text{Res}(f, z_0) = \frac{1}{(n-1)!} \lim_{z \to z_0} \frac{d^{n-1}}{dz^{n-1}} \left[ (z - z_0)^n f(z) \right]. \] In our case, \( n = 2 \), so \[ \text{Res}\left(\frac{2z^3 - 5z + 1}{(z - 1)^2}, 1\right) = \lim_{z \to 1} \frac{d}{dz} \left[ (z - 1)^2 \cdot \frac{2z^3 - 5z + 1}{(z - 1)^2} \right] = \lim_{z \to 1} \frac{d}{dz} (2z^3 - 5z + 1). \] Calculating the derivative, \[ \frac{d}{dz} (2z^3 - 5z + 1) = 6z^2 - 5. \] Evaluating at \( z = 1 \), \[ 6(1)^2 - 5 = 6 - 5 = 1. \] So, the residue at \( z = 1 \) is 1. Since this is the only singularity inside the contour \( |z| = 1 \), the integral evaluates to \[ \oint_C \frac{2z^3 - 5z + 1}{(z - 1)^2} \, dz = 2\pi i \times 1 = 2\pi i. \] Therefore, the value of the integral is \( 2\pi i \). </think> The value of the integral is \( 2\pi i \).

Evaluer fÃ¸lgende integral ved hjÃ¦lp af Cauchy Integral Formula: $ \ int_ {| z | = 1} \ frac {2z^3-5z+1} {(z-1)^2} \, dz $ Tip: Cauchy Integral Formel siger, at hvis $ F (z) $ er analytisk i en region, der indeholder en enkel, positivt orienteret lukket kontur $ C $ og hvis $ Z_0 $ er noget punktinteriÃ¸r til denne kontur, sÃ¥ $ \ oint_c \ frac {f (z)} {z-z_0} \, dz = 2 \ pi i f (z_0) $.
<think>Okay, jeg er nÃ¸dt til at evaluere integralet \ [ \ int_ {| z | = 1} \ frac {2z^3 - 5z + 1} {(z - 1)^2} \, dz \] Brug af Cauchy Integral Formula.Lad os fÃ¸rst huske, hvad Cauchy Integral Formel siger.Det siger, at hvis \ (f (z) \) er analytisk i en region, der indeholder et enkelt, positivt orienteret lukket kontur \ (c \), og hvis \ (z_0 \) er ethvert punkt interiÃ¸r til denne kontur, sÃ¥ \ [ \ oint_c \ frac {f (z)} {z - z_0} \, dz = 2 \ pi i f (z_0). \] I dette problem er vores kontur \ (C \) enhedens cirkel \ (| z | = 1 \).Vi er nÃ¸dt til at afgÃ¸re, om der er nogen singulariteter af integranden inde i denne kontur.Integrand er \ [ \ frac {2z^3 - 5z + 1} {(z - 1)^2}. \] NÃ¦vneren \ ((z - 1)^2 \) har en stang ved \ (z = 1 \).Nu er vi nÃ¸dt til at kontrollere, om denne pol ligger inde i eller uden for konturen \ (| z | = 1 \).Tilslutning af \ (z = 1 \), vi har \ (| 1 | = 1 \), sÃ¥ stangen er nÃ¸jagtigt pÃ¥ konturen.Imidlertid gÃ¦lder Cauchy Integral Formula, nÃ¥r singulariteten er ** inde ** konturen, ikke pÃ¥ den.Da \ (z = 1 \) ligger pÃ¥ konturen, kan vi derfor ikke direkte anvende standard Cauchy Integral Formula. Men vent, mÃ¥ske er der en mÃ¥de at justere for, at stangen er pÃ¥ konturen.MÃ¥ske kan vi i stedet bruge rest -sÃ¦tningen, der generaliserer Cauchy Integral Formula til at omfatte poler pÃ¥ konturen.RestsÃ¦ttelsen siger, at for en funktion med isolerede singulariteter inde i en simpel lukket kontur, \ [ \ oint_c f (z) \, dz = 2 \ pi i \ sum \ tekst {res} (f, z_k), \] hvor summen er over alle singulariteter \ (z_k \) inde \ (c \). Lad os fortsÃ¦tte med restsÃ¦tningen.Vores integrand har en dobbeltpol ved \ (z = 1 \).For at finde resterne ved denne pol skal vi beregne det fÃ¸rste derivat af tÃ¦lleren, der er evalueret ved \ (z = 1 \), da resterne for en pol af orden \ (n \) er givet af \ [ \ tekst {res} (f, z_0) = \ frac {1} {(n-1)!} \ lim_ {z \ til z_0} \ frac {d^{n-1}} {dz^{n-1}} \ venstre [(z-z_0)^n f (z) \ hÃ¸jre]. \] I vores tilfÃ¦lde \ (n = 2 \), sÃ¥ \ [ ov1)^2} \ hÃ¸jre] = \ lim_ {z \ til 1} \ frac {d} {dz} (2z^3 - 5z + 1). \] Beregning af derivatet, \ [ \ frac {d} {dz} (2z^3 - 5z + 1) = 6z^2 - 5. \] Evaluering ved \ (z = 1 \), \ [ 6 (1)^2 - 5 = 6 - 5 = 1. \] SÃ¥ resten ved \ (z = 1 \) er 1. Evalueer de volgende integraal met behulp van de Cauchy -integrale formule: $ \ int_ {| z | = 1} \ frac {2z^3-5z+1} {(z-1)^2} \, dz $ Hint: de Cauchy Integral-formule stelt dat als $ f (z) $ analytisch is in een regio met een eenvoudige, positief georiÃ«nteerde gesloten contour $ c $ en als $ z_0 $ een punt interieur is voor die contour, dan $ \ oint_c \ frac {f (z)} {z-z_0} \, dz = 2 \ pi i f (z_0) $.
<think>OkÃ©, ik moet de integraal evalueren \ [ \ int_ {| z | = 1} \ frac {2z^3 - 5z + 1} {(z - 1)^2} \, dz \] met behulp van de Cauchy -integrale formule.Laten we eerst herinneren wat de Cauchy -integrale formule stelt.Er staat dat als \ (f (z) \) analytisch is in een regio met een eenvoudige, positief georiÃ«nteerde gesloten contour \ (c \), en als \ (z_0 \) een punt is van die contour, dan \ [ \ oint_c \ frac {f (z)} {z - z_0} \, dz = 2 \ pi i f (z_0). \] In dit probleem is onze contour \ (c \) de eenheidscirkel \ (| z | = 1 \).We moeten bepalen of er in deze contour singulariteiten van het integrand zijn.De integrand is \ [ \ frac {2z^3 - 5z + 1} {(z - 1)^2}. \] De noemer \ ((z - 1)^2 \) heeft een pool op \ (z = 1 \).Nu moeten we controleren of deze paal binnen of buiten de contour \ (| z | = 1 \) ligt.Inpluggen \ (z = 1 \), hebben we \ (| 1 | = 1 \), dus de paal staat precies op de contour.De Cauchy -integrale formule is echter van toepassing wanneer de singulariteit ** in de contour is, niet erop.Aangezien \ (z = 1 \) op de contour ligt, kunnen we daarom de standaard Cauchy -integrale formule rechtstreeks toepassen. Maar wacht, misschien is er een manier om zich aan te passen dat de paal op de contour staat.Misschien kunnen we in plaats daarvan de residu -stelling gebruiken, die de Cauchy -integrale formule generaliseert om polen op de contour op te nemen.De residu -stelling stelt dat voor een functie met geÃ¯soleerde singulariteiten in een eenvoudige gesloten contour, \ [ \ oint_c f (z) \, dz = 2 \ pi i \ sum \ text {res} (f, z_k), \] waar de som over alle singulariteiten is \ (z_k \) in \ (c \). Laten we doorgaan met de stelling van de residu.Onze integrand heeft een dubbele paal op \ (z = 1 \).Om het residu op deze paal te vinden, moeten we de eerste afgeleide van de getal geÃ«valueerd op \ (z = 1 \) berekenen, omdat het residu voor een pool van orde \ (n \) wordt gegeven door \ [ \ text {res} (f, z_0) = \ frac {1} {(n-1)!} \ lim_ {z \ to z_0} \ frac {d^{n-1}} {dz^{n-1}} \ left [(z-z_0)^n f (z) \ rechter]. \] In ons geval \ (n = 2 \), dus \ [ \ text {res} \ links (\ frac {2z^3 - 5z + 1} {(z - 1)^2}, 1 \ rechts) = \ lim_ {z \ tot 1} \ frac {d} {dz} \ links [(z - 1)^2 \ 2 \ cdot \ cdot \ 2z^3 - 5z + 1} {2}\ rechts] = \ lim_ {z \ tot 1} \ frac {d} {dz} (2z^3 - 5z + 1). \] Het berekenen van de afgeleide, \ [ \ frac {d} {dz} (2z^3 - 5z + 1) = 6Z^2 - 5. \] Evalueren op \ (z = 1 \), \ [ 6 (1)^2 - 5 = 6 - 5 = 1. \] Dus het residu op \ (z = 1 \) is 1. omdat dit de enige singulariteit is in de contour \ (| z | = 1 \), evalueert de integrale \ [ \ oint_c \ frac {2z^3 - 5z + 1} {(z - 1)^2} \, dz = 2 \ pi i \ maal 1 = 2 \ pi i. \] Daarom is de waarde van de integrale \ (2 \ pi i \).</think><Output>De waarde van de integrale is \ (2 \ pi i \).</Output>

Bewerten Sie das folgende Integral mit der Cauchy -Integralformel: $ \ int_ {| z | = 1} \ frac {2z^3-5z+1} {(z-1)^2} \, dz $ Hinweis: In der Cauchy-Integral-Formel heiÃŸt es, dass $ f (z) $ in einer Region mit einer einfachen, positiv ausgerichteten geschlossenen Kontur $ C $ analytisch ist und wenn $ z_0 $ ein Punkt in diesem Kontur ist, dann $ \ opt_c \ frac {f (z) {z-z_0} \ \ \, dz = 2 \ pi i f (z_0 $).
<think>Okay, ich muss das Integral bewerten \ [ \ int_ {| z | = 1} \ frac {2z^3 - 5z + 1} {(z - 1)^2} \, dz \] Verwenden der Cauchy Integral -Formel.Erinnern wir uns zunÃ¤chst, wie die Cauchy -Integralformel sagt.Es heiÃŸt, wenn \ (f (z) \) in einem Bereich analysiert ist, der eine einfache, positiv orientierte geschlossene Kontur \ (c \) enthÃ¤lt, und wenn \ (z_0 \) ein Punkt in dieser Kontur ist \ [ \ oint_c \ frac {f (z)} {z - z_0} \, dz = 2 \ pi i f (z_0). \] In diesem Problem ist unsere Kontur \ (c \) der Einheitskreis \ (| z | = 1 \).Wir mÃ¼ssen feststellen, ob es in dieser Kontur SingularitÃ¤ten des Integrals gibt.Das Integrand ist \ [ \ frac {2z^3 - 5z + 1} {(z - 1)^2}. \] Der Nenner \ ((z - 1)^2 \) hat einen Pol bei \ (z = 1 \).Jetzt mÃ¼ssen wir Ã¼berprÃ¼fen, ob diese Pole innerhalb oder auÃŸerhalb der Kontur \ (| z | = 1 \) liegt.Wenn wir \ (z = 1 \) einstecken, haben wir \ (| 1 | = 1 \), also ist der Pol genau auf der Kontur.Die Cauchy -Integral -Formel gilt jedoch, wenn die SingularitÃ¤t in der Kontur ist, nicht darauf.Da \ (z = 1 \) auf der Kontur liegt, kÃ¶nnen wir die Standard -Cauchy -Integralformel nicht direkt anwenden. Aber warte, vielleicht gibt es eine MÃ¶glichkeit, sich an die Stange auf der Kontur anzupassen.Vielleicht kÃ¶nnen wir stattdessen den RÃ¼ckstandsatz verwenden, der die Cauchy -Integral -Formel so verallgemeinert, dass Pole auf der Kontur einbezogen werden.Der RÃ¼ckstandsatz besagt, dass fÃ¼r eine Funktion mit isolierten SingularitÃ¤ten innerhalb einer einfachen geschlossenen Kontur, \ [ \ oint_c f (z) \, dz = 2 \ pi i \ sum \ text {res} (f, z_k), \] wobei die Summe Ã¼ber alle SingularitÃ¤ten \ (z_k \) in \ (c \) liegt. Machen wir mit dem RÃ¼ckstandsatz fort.Unser Integrand hat einen Doppelpol bei \ (z = 1 \).Um den RÃ¼ckstand an diesem Pol zu finden, mÃ¼ssen wir die erste Ableitung des bei \ (z = 1 \) bewerteten ZÃ¤hlers berechnen, da der Rest fÃ¼r einen Pole der Ordnung \ (n \) gegeben ist durch \ [ \ text {res} (f, z_0) = \ frac {1} {(n-1)!} \ lim_ {z \ to z_0} \ frac {d^{n-1}} {dz^{n-1} \ links [(z-z_0)^n f (z) \ right]. \] In unserem Fall \ (n = 2 \), so \ [ \text{Res}\left(\frac{2z^3 - 5z + 1}{(z - 1)^2}, 1\right) = \lim_{z \to 1} \frac{d}{dz} \left[ (z - 1)^2 \cdot \frac{2z^3 - 5z + 1}{(z - 1)^2}\ right] = \ lim_ {z \ bis 1} \ frac {d} {dz} (2z^3 - 5z + 1). \] Berechnung des Derivats, \ [ \ frac {d} {dz} (2z^3 - 5z + 1) = 6z^2 - 5. \] Bewertung bei \ (z = 1 \), \ [ 6 (1)^2 - 5 = 6 - 5 = 1. \] Der RÃ¼ckstand bei \ (z = 1 \) betrÃ¤gt also 1. Da dies die einzige SingularitÃ¤t in der Kontur \ (| z | = 1 \) ist, bewertet das Integral an \ [ \ oint_c \ frac {2z^3 - 5z + 1} {(z - 1)^2} \, dz = 2 \ pi i \ times 1 = 2 \ pi i. \] Daher ist der Wert des Integrals \ (2 \ pi i \).</think><Output>Der Wert des Integrals ist \ (2 \ pi i \).</Output>

Valuta il seguente integrale utilizzando la formula integrale Cauchy: $ \ int_ {| z | = 1} \ frac {2z^3-5z+1} {(z-1)^2} \, dz $ Suggerimento: la formula integrale Cauchy afferma che se $ f (z) $ Ã¨ analitico in una regione contenente un contorno chiuso semplice, orientato positivamente $ c $ e se $ z_0 $ Ã¨ un punto interno a quel contorno, allora $ \ oint_c \ frac {f (z)} {z-zz_0} \, dz = 2 \ pi i f (z_0) $.

<think>OK, jeg mÃ¥ evaluere integralen \ [ \ int_ {| z | = 1} \ frac {2z^3 - 5z + 1} {(z - 1)^2} \, dz \] ved hjelp av Cauchy Integral Formula.La oss fÃ¸rst huske hva Cauchy integrerte formel sier.Den sier at hvis \ (f (z) \) er analytisk i en region som inneholder en enkel, positivt orientert lukket kontur \ (c \), og hvis \ (z_0 \) er et hvilket \ [ \ Oint_C \ frac {f (z)} {z - z_0} \, dz = 2 \ pi i f (z_0). \] I dette problemet er vÃ¥r kontur \ (c \) enhetssirkelen \ (| z | = 1 \).Vi mÃ¥ avgjÃ¸re om det er noen singulariteter i integranden i denne konturen.Integranden er \ [ \ frac {2z^3 - 5z + 1} {(z - 1)^2}. \] Nevneren \ ((z - 1)^2 \) har en stolpe ved \ (z = 1 \).NÃ¥ mÃ¥ vi sjekke om denne polen ligger i eller utenfor konturen \ (| z | = 1 \).Plugging til \ (z = 1 \), har vi \ (| 1 | = 1 \), sÃ¥ polen er nÃ¸yaktig pÃ¥ konturen.Imidlertid gjelder den cauchy integrerte formelen nÃ¥r singulariteten er ** inni ** konturen, ikke pÃ¥ den.Siden \ (z = 1 \) ligger pÃ¥ konturen, kan vi derfor ikke direkte bruke standard Cauchy integrerte formel. Men vent, kanskje det er en mÃ¥te Ã¥ justere for at polen er pÃ¥ konturen.Kanskje vi i stedet kan bruke reststeoremet, som generaliserer Cauchy integrerte formel for Ã¥ inkludere poler pÃ¥ konturen.Restteoremet sier at for en funksjon med isolerte singulariteter inne i en enkel lukket kontur, \ [ \ Oint_C F (Z) \, DZ = 2 \ PI I \ SUM \ Tekst {Res} (F, Z_K), \] der summen er over alle singulariteter \ (z_k \) inne \ (c \). La oss fortsette med reststeoremet.Integranden vÃ¥r har en dobbeltstang ved \ (z = 1 \).For Ã¥ finne resten ved denne polen, mÃ¥ vi beregne det fÃ¸rste derivatet av telleren som er evaluert ved \ (z = 1 \), siden resten for en stang av orden \ (n \) er gitt av \ [ \ text {res} (f, z_0) = \ frac {1} {(n-1)!} \ lim_ {z \ til z_0} \ frac {d^{n-1}} {dz^{n-1}} \ venstre [(z-z_0)^n f (z)} \ \. \] I vÃ¥rt tilfelle, \ (n = 2 \), sÃ¥ \ [ \ tekst {res} \ venstre (\ frac {2z^3 - 5z + 1} {(z - 1)^2}, 1 \ hÃ¸yre) = \ lim_ {z \ til 1} \ frac {d} {dz} \ venstre [(z - 1)^2 {(z -1)^2} \ hÃ¸yre] = \ lim_ {z \ til 1} \ frac {d} {dz} (2z^3 - 5z + 1). \] Beregne derivatet, \ [ \ frac {d} {dz} (2z^3 - 5z + 1) = 6z^2 - 5. \] Evaluering av ved \ (z = 1 \), \ [ 6 (1)^2 - 5 = 6 - 5 = 1. \] SÃ¥ resten ved \ (z = 1 \) er 1. Siden dette er den eneste singulariteten inne i konturen \ (| z | = 1 \), evaluerer integral \ [ \ Oint_C \ frac {2z^3 - 5z + 1} {(z - 1)^2} \, dz = 2 \ pi i \ ganger 1 = 2 \ pi i. \] Derfor er verdien av integralen \ (2 \ pi i \).</think><Output>Verdien av integralen er \ (2 \ pi i \).</Output>

Vamos prosseguir com o teorema de resÃ­duos.Nosso integrando tem um pÃ³lo duplo em \ (z = 1 \).Para encontrar o resÃ­duo neste poste, precisaremos calcular a primeira derivada do numerador avaliado em \ (z = 1 \), uma vez que o resÃ­duo para um polo de ordem \ (n \) Ã© dado por \ [[ \ text {res} (f, z_0) = \ frac {1} {(n-1)!} \ lim_ {z \ to z_0} \ frac {d^{n-1}} {dz^{n-1} \ esquerda [(z-z_0)^n f (z) {n-1}} \ esquerda [(z_0)^n) {. \] No nosso caso, \ (n = 2 \), entÃ£o \ [[ \text{Res}\left(\frac{2z^3 - 5z + 1}{(z - 1)^2}, 1\right) = \lim_{z \to 1} \frac{d}{dz} \left[ (z - 1)^2 \cdot \frac{2z^3 - 5z + 1}{(z - 1)^2}\ direita] = \ lim_ {z \ a 1} \ frac {d} {dz} (2z^3 - 5z + 1). \] Calculando o derivado, \ [[ \ frac {d} {dz} (2z^3 - 5z + 1) = 6z^2 - 5. \] AvaliaÃ§Ã£o em \ (z = 1 \), \ [[ 6 (1)^2 - 5 = 6 - 5 = 1. \] Portanto, o resÃ­duo em \ (z = 1 \) Ã© 1. EvalÃºe la siguiente integral utilizando la fÃ³rmula integral de Cauchy: $ \ int_ {| z | = 1} \ frac {2z^3-5z+1} {(z-1)^2} \, dz $ Sugerencia: la fÃ³rmula integral de Cauchy establece que si $ f (z) $ es analÃ­tico en una regiÃ³n que contiene un contorno cerrado simple y orientado positivamente $ C $ y si $ z_0 $ es cualquier punto interior a ese contorno, entonces $ \ oint_c \ frac {f (z)} {z-z_0} \, dz = 2 \ pi I f (z__0) $.
<think>Muy bien, necesito evaluar la integral \ [ \ int_ {| z | = 1} \ frac {2z^3 - 5z + 1} {(z - 1)^2} \, dz \] Usando la fÃ³rmula integral de Cauchy.Primero, recordemos lo que dice la fÃ³rmula integral de Cauchy.Dice que si \ (f (z) \) es analÃ­tico en una regiÃ³n que contiene un contorno cerrado simple y orientado positivamente \ (c \), y si \ (z_0 \) es cualquier punto interior a ese contorno, entonces \ [ \ oint_c \ frac {f (z)} {z - z_0} \, dz = 2 \ pi i f (z_0). \] En este problema, nuestro contorno \ (c \) es el cÃ­rculo unitario \ (| z | = 1 \).Necesitamos determinar si hay singularidades del integrando dentro de este contorno.El integrando es \ [ \ frac {2z^3 - 5z + 1} {(z - 1)^2}. \] El denominador \ ((z - 1)^2 \) tiene un polo en \ (z = 1 \).Ahora, necesitamos verificar si este polo se encuentra dentro o fuera del contorno \ (| z | = 1 \).Conectando \ (z = 1 \), tenemos \ (| 1 | = 1 \), por lo que el polo estÃ¡ exactamente en el contorno.Sin embargo, la fÃ³rmula integral de Cauchy se aplica cuando la singularidad estÃ¡ ** dentro ** el contorno, no en ella.Por lo tanto, dado que \ (z = 1 \) se encuentra en el contorno, no podemos aplicar directamente la fÃ³rmula integral de Cauchy estÃ¡ndar. Pero espera, tal vez hay una manera de ajustar para que el poste estÃ© en el contorno.QuizÃ¡s podamos usar el teorema de residuos, lo que generaliza la fÃ³rmula integral de Cauchy para incluir postes en el contorno.El teorema de los residuos establece que para una funciÃ³n con singularidades aisladas dentro de un simple contorno cerrado, \ [ \ oint_c f (z) \, dz = 2 \ pi i \ sum \ text {res} (f, z_k), \] donde la suma se trata de todas las singularidades \ (z_k \) dentro \ (c \). Proceda con el teorema de residuos.Nuestro integrando tiene un polo doble en \ (z = 1 \).Para encontrar el residuo en este polo, necesitaremos calcular la primera derivada del numerador evaluado en \ (z = 1 \), ya que el residuo para un polo de orden \ (n \) estÃ¡ dado por \ [ \ Text {res} (f, z_0) = \ frac {1} {(n-1)!} \ lim_ {z \ a z_0} \ frac {d^{n-1}} {dz^{n-1}} \ izquierdo [(z-z_0)^n f (z) \ correcto]. \] En nuestro caso, \ (n = 2 \), entonces \ [ \ text {res} \ izquierda (\ frac {2z^3 - 5z + 1} {(z - 1)^2}, 1 \ right) = \ lim_ {z \ a 1} \ frac {d} {dz} \ izquierda [(z - 1)^2 \ cdot \ frac {2Z^3 - 5Z + 1} {(z - 1)^2} \\ a 1} \ frac {d} {dz} (2z^3 - 5z + 1). \] Calculando la derivada, \ [ \ frac {d} {dz} (2z^3 - 5z + 1) = 6z^2 - 5. \] Evaluando en \ (z = 1 \), \ [ 6 (1)^2 - 5 = 6 - 5 = 1. \] Entonces, el residuo en \ (z = 1 \) es 1. Dado que esta es la Ãºnica singularidad dentro del contorno \ (| z | = 1 \), la integral evalÃºa a \ [ \ oint_c \ frac {2z^3 - 5z + 1} {(z - 1)^2} \, dz = 2 \ pi i \ Times 1 = 2 \ pi i. \] Por lo tanto, el valor de la integral es \ (2 \ pi I \).</think><Output>El valor de la integral es \ (2 \ pi I \).</Output>

UtvÃ¤rdera fÃ¶ljande integral med hjÃ¤lp av Cauchy -integrerad formel: $ \ int_ {| z | = 1} \ frac {2z^3-5z+1} {(z-1)^2} \, dz $ Hint: The Cauchy Integral Formula states that if $f(z)$ is analytic in a region containing a simple, positively oriented closed contour $C$ and if $z_0$ is any point interior to that contour, then $\oint_C \frac{f(z)}{z-z_0} \,dz = 2\pi i f(z_0)$.
<think>Okej, jag mÃ¥ste utvÃ¤rdera det integrerade \ [ \ int_ {| z | = 1} \ frac {2z^3 - 5z + 1} {(z - 1)^2} \, dz \] med hjÃ¤lp av Cauchy -integrerad formel.LÃ¥t oss fÃ¶rst komma ihÃ¥g vad Cauchy -integrerade formeln sÃ¤ger.Den sÃ¤ger att om \ (f (z) \) Ã¤r analytisk i en region som innehÃ¥ller en enkel, positivt orienterad stÃ¤ngd kontur \ (c \), och om \ (z_0 \) Ã¤r nÃ¥gon punkt inre till den konturen, dÃ¥ \ [ \ oint_c \ frac {f (z)} {z - z_0} \, dz = 2 \ pi i f (z_0). \] I detta problem Ã¤r vÃ¥r kontur \ (c \) enhetscirkeln \ (| z | = 1 \).Vi mÃ¥ste avgÃ¶ra om det finns nÃ¥gra singulariteter i integranden i denna kontur.Integrand Ã¤r \ [ \ frac {2z^3 - 5z + 1} {(z - 1)^2}. \] NÃ¤mnaren \ ((z - 1)^2 \) har en stolpe vid \ (z = 1 \).Nu mÃ¥ste vi kontrollera om denna stolpe ligger inom eller utanfÃ¶r konturen \ (| z | = 1 \).Plugging \ (z = 1 \), vi har \ (| 1 | = 1 \), sÃ¥ polen Ã¤r exakt pÃ¥ konturen.Cauchy -integrerad formel gÃ¤ller emellertid nÃ¤r singulariteten Ã¤r ** inuti ** konturen, inte pÃ¥ den.DÃ¤rfÃ¶r, eftersom \ (z = 1 \) ligger pÃ¥ konturen, kan vi inte direkt tillÃ¤mpa standard Cauchy -integrerad formel. Men vÃ¤nta, kanske finns det ett sÃ¤tt att anpassa sig till polen som Ã¤r pÃ¥ konturen.Kanske kan vi anvÃ¤nda Ã¥terstodensteoremet istÃ¤llet, vilket generaliserar Cauchy -integrerad formel fÃ¶r att inkludera poler pÃ¥ konturen.Ã…terstoden satsen sÃ¤ger att fÃ¶r en funktion med isolerade singulariteter i en enkel stÃ¤ngd kontur, \ [ \ oint_c f (z) \, dz = 2 \ pi i \ sum \ text {res} (f, z_k), \] dÃ¤r summan Ã¤r Ã¶ver alla singulariteter \ (z_k \) inuti \ (c \). LÃ¥t oss fortsÃ¤tta med reststeoremet.VÃ¥r integrand har en dubbelpol vid \ (z = 1 \).FÃ¶r att hitta Ã¥terstoden vid denna pol mÃ¥ste vi berÃ¤kna det fÃ¶rsta derivatet av telleren utvÃ¤rderat vid \ (z = 1 \), eftersom Ã¥terstoden fÃ¶r en ordstÃ¥ng \ (n \) ges av \ [ \ text {res} (f, z_0) = \ frac {1} {(n-1)!} \ lim_ {z \ till z_0} \ frac {d^{n-1} {dz^{n-1} \ vÃ¤nster [(z-z_0)^n f (z) \ hÃ¶ger]. \] I vÃ¥rt fall \ (n = 2 \), sÃ¥ \ [ \ text {res} \ vÃ¤nster (\ frac {2z^3 - 5z + 1} {(z - 1)^2}, 1 \ hÃ¶ger) = \ lim_ {z \ till 1} \ frac {d} {dz \ \ vÃ¤nster [(z - 1)^2 \ cDot \ \ \ \\ hÃ¶ger] = \ lim_ {z \ till 1} \ frac {d} {dz} (2z^3 - 5z + 1). \] BerÃ¤kna derivatet, \ [ \ frac {d} {dz} (2z^3 - 5z + 1) = 6z^2 - 5. \] UtvÃ¤rdera vid \ (z = 1 \), \ [ 6 (1)^2 - 5 = 6 - 5 = 1. \] SÃ¥ Ã¥terstoden vid \ (z = 1 \) Ã¤r 1. Eftersom detta Ã¤r den enda singulariteten inuti konturen \ (| z | = 1 \), utvÃ¤rderas den integrerade till \ [ \ oint_c \ frac {2z^3 - 5z + 1} {(z - 1)^2} \, dz = 2 \ pi i \ gÃ¥nger 1 = 2 \ pi i. \] DÃ¤rfÃ¶r Ã¤r vÃ¤rdet pÃ¥ integralen \ (2 \ pi i \).</think><Output>VÃ¤rdet pÃ¥ integralen Ã¤r \ (2 \ pi i \).</Output>

en
Ryan works in an office that has an even number of men and women working there. Ryan participates in a meeting composed of 4 men and 6 women who are pulled from the office floor. This reduces the number of women working on the office floor by 20%. How many people work at Ryan's office?
<think> Alright, let's tackle this problem step by step to determine how many people work at Ryan's office. First, we know that the office has an even number of men and women. Let's denote the number of men as M and the number of women as W. Since the total number of employees is even, both M and W must be even numbers. Next, Ryan participates in a meeting that consists of 4 men and 6 women. This meeting is pulled from the office floor. After this meeting, the number of women working on the office floor decreases by 20%. Let's break down the information: 1. **Initial Number of Women:** - Before the meeting, there are W women working on the floor. - After the meeting, the number of women decreases by 20%. - So, the remaining number of women after the meeting is 80% of W, which can be written as 0.8W. 2. **Number of Women in the Meeting:** - The meeting includes 6 women. - Therefore, the number of women remaining on the floor is W - 6. - According to the first point, W - 6 = 0.8W. 3. **Setting Up the Equation:** - From the above, we have: \[ W - 6 = 0.8W \] - To solve for W, subtract 0.8W from both sides: \[ W - 0.8W = 6 \\ 0.2W = 6 \] - Now, divide both sides by 0.2: \[ W = \frac{6}{0.2} \\ W = 30 \] 4. **Determining the Number of Men:** - Since the total number of employees is even and there are W = 30 women, the number of men M must also be even. - However, the problem doesn't provide direct information about the number of men, but it states that the office has an even number of men and women. - Given that W = 30 (which is even), M must also be even. But without additional constraints or information, M could be any even number that complements W to form an even total number of employees. 5. **Calculating the Total Number of Employees:** - The total number of employees is M + W. - Since W = 30, the total becomes M + 30. - Without knowing the exact number of men, we cannot determine the precise total number of employees. 6. **Possible Scenarios:** - If we assume that the number of men is equal to the number of women (which might not necessarily be the case, but it's a common assumption for such problems), then M = 30. - Therefore, the total number of employees would be 30 (men) + 30 (women) = 60. 7. **Conclusion:** - Based on the given information and assuming that the number of men equals the number of women, the total number of employees at Ryan's office is 60. </think> 60
